\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ "{}u8x8.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ following\ macro\ enables\ 16\ Bit\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Without\ defining\ this\ macro\ all\ calculations\ are\ done\ with\ 8\ Bit\ (1\ Byte)\ variables.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Especially\ on\ AVR\ architecture,\ this\ will\ save\ some\ space.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ If\ this\ macro\ is\ defined,\ then\ U8g2\ will\ switch\ to\ 16\ Bit\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Use\ 16\ Bit\ mode\ for\ any\ display\ with\ more\ than\ 240\ pixel\ in\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_16BIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ always\ enable\ U8G2\_16BIT\ on\ 32bit\ environments,\ see\ issue\ https://github.com/olikraus/u8g2/issues/1222\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_16BIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(unix)\ ||\ defined(\_\_unix\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_arm\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_xtensa\_\_)\ ||\ defined(xtensa)\ ||\ defined(\_\_arc\_\_)\ ||\ defined(ESP8266)\ ||\ defined(ESP\_PLATFORM)\ ||\ defined(\_\_LUATOS\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_16BIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ following\ macro\ switches\ the\ library\ into\ dynamic\ display\ buffer\ allocation\ mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Defining\ this\ constant\ will\ disable\ all\ static\ memory\ allocation\ for\ device\ memory\ buffer\ and\ thus\ allows\ the\ user\ to\ allocate\ device\ buffers\ statically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Before\ using\ any\ display\ functions,\ the\ dynamic\ buffer\ *must*\ be\ assigned\ to\ the\ u8g2\ struct\ using\ the\ u8g2\_SetBufferPtr\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ When\ using\ dynamic\ allocation,\ the\ stack\ size\ must\ be\ increased\ by\ u8g2\_GetBufferSize\ bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \#define\ U8G2\_USE\_DYNAMIC\_ALLOC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ U8g2\ feature\ selection,\ see\ also\ https://github.com/olikraus/u8g2/wiki/u8g2optimization\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ following\ macro\ enables\ the\ HVLine\ speed\ optimization.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ It\ will\ consume\ about\ 40\ bytes\ more\ in\ flash\ memory\ of\ the\ AVR.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ HVLine\ procedures\ are\ also\ used\ by\ the\ text\ drawing\ functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_WITHOUT\_HVLINE\_SPEED\_OPTIMIZATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_WITH\_HVLINE\_SPEED\_OPTIMIZATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ following\ macro\ activates\ the\ early\ intersection\ check\ with\ the\ current\ visible\ area.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Clipping\ (and\ low\ level\ intersection\ calculation)\ will\ still\ happen\ and\ is\ controlled\ by\ U8G2\_WITH\_CLIPPING.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ This\ early\ intersection\ check\ only\ improves\ speed\ for\ the\ picture\ loop\ (u8g2\_FirstPage/NextPage).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ With\ a\ full\ framebuffer\ in\ RAM\ and\ if\ most\ graphical\ elements\ are\ drawn\ within\ the\ visible\ area,\ then\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ macro\ can\ be\ commented\ to\ reduce\ code\ size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_WITHOUT\_INTERSECTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_WITH\_INTERSECTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Enable\ clip\ window\ support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ void\ u8g2\_SetMaxClipWindow(u8g2\_t\ *u8g2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ void\ u8g2\_SetClipWindow(u8g2\_t\ *u8g2,\ u8g2\_uint\_t\ clip\_x0,\ u8g2\_uint\_t\ clip\_y0,\ u8g2\_uint\_t\ clip\_x1,\ u8g2\_uint\_t\ clip\_y1\ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Setting\ a\ clip\ window\ will\ restrict\ all\ drawing\ to\ this\ window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Clip\ window\ support\ requires\ about\ 200\ bytes\ flash\ memory\ on\ AVR\ systems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_WITHOUT\_CLIP\_WINDOW\_SUPPORT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_WITH\_CLIP\_WINDOW\_SUPPORT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ following\ macro\ enables\ all\ four\ drawing\ directions\ for\ glyphs\ and\ strings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ If\ this\ macro\ is\ not\ defined,\ than\ a\ string\ can\ be\ drawn\ only\ in\ horizontal\ direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Jan\ 2020:\ Disabling\ this\ macro\ will\ save\ up\ to\ 600\ bytes\ on\ AVR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_WITHOUT\_FONT\_ROTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_WITH\_FONT\_ROTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ U8glib\ V2\ contains\ support\ for\ unicode\ plane\ 0\ (Basic\ Multilingual\ Plane,\ BMP).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ following\ macro\ activates\ this\ support.\ Deactivation\ would\ save\ some\ ROM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ This\ definition\ also\ defines\ the\ behavior\ of\ the\ expected\ string\ encoding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ If\ the\ following\ macro\ is\ defined,\ then\ the\ DrawUTF8\ function\ is\ enabled\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ the\ string\ argument\ for\ this\ function\ is\ assumed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ to\ be\ UTF-\/8\ encoded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ If\ the\ following\ macro\ is\ not\ defined,\ then\ all\ strings\ in\ the\ c-\/code\ are\ assumed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ to\ be\ ISO\ 8859-\/1/CP1252\ encoded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Independently\ from\ this\ macro,\ the\ Arduino\ print\ function\ never\ accepts\ UTF-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ strings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ This\ macro\ does\ not\ affect\ the\ u8x8\ string\ draw\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ u8x8\ has\ also\ two\ function,\ one\ for\ pure\ strings\ and\ one\ for\ UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Conclusion:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ U8G2\_WITH\_UNICODE\ defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ C-\/Code\ Strings\ must\ be\ UTF-\/8\ encoded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Full\ support\ of\ all\ 65536\ glyphs\ of\ the\ unicode\ basic\ multilingual\ plane}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Up\ to\ 65536\ glyphs\ of\ the\ font\ file\ can\ be\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ U8G2\_WITH\_UNICODE\ not\ defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ C-\/Code\ Strings\ are\ assumbed\ to\ be\ ISO\ 8859-\/1/CP1252\ encoded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Only\ character\ values\ 0\ to\ 255\ are\ supported\ in\ the\ font\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_WITHOUT\_UNICODE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_WITH\_UNICODE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ See\ issue\ https://github.com/olikraus/u8g2/issues/1561}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ old\ behaviour\ of\ the\ StrWidth\ and\ UTF8Width\ functions\ returned\ an\ unbalanced\ string\ width,\ where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ a\ small\ space\ was\ added\ to\ the\ left\ but\ not\ to\ the\ right\ of\ the\ string\ in\ some\ cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ The\ new\ "{}balanced"{}\ procedure\ will\ assume\ the\ same\ gap\ on\ the\ left\ and\ the\ right\ side\ of\ the\ string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Example:\ The\ string\ width\ of\ "{}C"{}\ with\ font\ u8g2\_font\_helvR08\_tr\ was\ returned\ as\ 7.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ A\ frame\ of\ width\ 9\ would\ place\ the\ C\ a\ little\ bit\ more\ to\ the\ right\ (width\ of\ that\ "{}C"{}\ are\ 6\ pixel).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ If\ U8G2\_BALANCED\_STR\_WIDTH\_CALCULATION\ is\ defined,\ the\ width\ of\ "{}C"{}\ is\ returned\ as\ 8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Not\ defining\ U8G2\_BALANCED\_STR\_WIDTH\_CALCULATION\ would\ fall\ back\ to\ the\ old\ behavior.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ U8G2\_NO\_BALANCED\_STR\_WIDTH\_CALCULATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ U8G2\_BALANCED\_STR\_WIDTH\_CALCULATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{/*==========================================*/}}
